| 0:28:30| If people have refuse collection at the curb, then in order to have high participation,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/citycouncilworkshop091210?start=1710)|
| 0:28:34| you need to give them recycling collection at the curb, preferably on the same day.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/citycouncilworkshop091210?start=1714)|

| 0:28:44| paper together into the same container so that they don't have to have a bag for white| [source video](https://archive.org/details/citycouncilworkshop091210?start=1724)|

| 0:28:59| Trash volume carts, when we first started recycling 20, 30 years ago, we were giving| [source video](https://archive.org/details/citycouncilworkshop091210?start=1739)|
| 0:29:04| everyone the little blue bin, and that was great back then, but if you think about how| [source video](https://archive.org/details/citycouncilworkshop091210?start=1744)|

| 0:47:23| And Mayor Haslam had asked, you know, Mr. Wetzel and I, really towards the end of his first term, to look at recycling because he'd had requests about curbside.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/citycouncilworkshop091210?start=2843)|
| 0:47:32| There was more discussion about it.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/citycouncilworkshop091210?start=2852)|
| 0:47:34| And from a sustainability standpoint, how can we divert more materials long-term from landfills?| [source video](https://archive.org/details/citycouncilworkshop091210?start=2854)|
| 0:47:39| That's really why we're here today was those two questions we wanted to be able to ask.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/citycouncilworkshop091210?start=2859)|
| 0:47:43| If we want to go to the next level, we have to make it as easy to throw out the material that you're going to recycle as your garbage.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/citycouncilworkshop091210?start=2863)|
| 0:47:49| You've got to have two bins.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/citycouncilworkshop091210?start=2869)|
| 0:47:50| You just throw it in.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/citycouncilworkshop091210?start=2870)|
| 0:47:51| And that's how you start to get up to 50 and 60 percent participation rates.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/citycouncilworkshop091210?start=2871)|
| 0:47:56| One note on the 8 percent recycling rate, that does not include our yard waste.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/citycouncilworkshop091210?start=2876)|

| 0:48:04| That does not go to the landfill.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/citycouncilworkshop091210?start=2884)|

| 0:48:13| which is kudos for us from a sustainability standpoint.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/citycouncilworkshop091210?start=2893)|

| 0:48:18| I just want to add on.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/citycouncilworkshop091210?start=2898)|
